Important info for suppliers and clients:
Before we sign any contract, you must have a medical certificate that shows you have the mental capacity / discernment / legal competence to sign documents, and you must be over 21.
( e.g. Some people are underage or they are very old or sick. These people are not allowed to sign contracts )

A. We do not sell or offer services to private persons. ( We are a B2B company )
B. We do not store products, we buy the products from suppliers after clients sign contracts and send payment.
C. This way clients will get the products fresh, and we will reduce energy and storage costs.
D. We will buy from suppliers fresh products only. You should not manufacture products without a contract.

Grocery List ( Click Here To Copy )


    How To Buy Guide

    Edit the grocery list and add quantity you need for each BSEI code

    You can use LibraOffice Calc, Excel, Word

    ( e.g. BSEI-100119-0001 x 1000 tonnes )


    1. Send grocery list via E-mail or Whatsapp

    2. We verify your company public documents

    3. You send technical specs for each product

    4. We verify if products can be sent to you

    5. We request prices from suppliers

    6. We select the best prices from suppliers

    7. We send you the best prices


    If your happy with the prices

    8. We prepare commission contract clauses, shipping and itinerary ( and export-import procedures for non-EU countries ).

    9. The commission fee is 10% out of Total costs. Total costs you will see in the estimative costs annex of the contract.

    10. We and the banks check the documents, and we sign contract, We send you the proforma invoice and your company has to transfer the payment via TT / Money Order ( Bank Transfer ).

    11. We start he delivery process after payment is confirmed, we also send you copy of legal invoice - payment receipt.

    12. Suppliers will be paid after you inspect the products when they arrive at your location and after you sign the handover documents. ( Why ? Do to fact suppliers are sneaky, they use sweet talk to get contracts, and after they do bad work or deliver junk products. )

    13. If the products are not according to contract terms, we will refund you the money minus expenses included in the contract.

    14. If suppliers do not respect contract terms, they get zero payment.


    Example of Total costs:

    Suppliers scouting price on invoice ( bus-plane tickets, food, room rent, visa etc ) : $1000
    Packaging design, label design, trademark registration in USA price on invoice: $3000
    Raw materials Laboratory analysis price on invoice: $500
    Documents translation and lawyers price on invoice: $500
    Romania and USA import-export licences and government authorizations price on invoice: $500
    Almost 10-15year documents archiving price on invoice: $500
    Product 1 manufacturing price on invoice: 100pcs x $10 = $1000
    Product 2 manufacturing price on invoice: 1000pcs x $10 = $10000
    Product 3 manufacturing price on invoice: 100pcs x $10 = S1000
    Quality control finate products laboratory analysis fees: $1500
    Products compliance with EU and USA standards ( e.g. CE marking documents ) price on invoice: $5000
    Certificate of Origin price on invoice: $500
    40FT Container Rent Focsani - New York price on invoice: $3000
    Warehousing, Logistics, labeling and packaging price on invoice: $5000
    Transport Focsani - New York price on invoice: $10000
    Export Insurance price on invoice: $1000
    Romania and USA Customs brokers price on invoice: $10000
    VAT and Customs Taxes invoice: $10000
    Accounting price on invoice: $5000
    Romania and USA Products security and monitoring price on invoice: $5000
    Corporate intelligence price on invoice: $3000
    Communication and IT services price on invoice ( e.g. Romania to USA phone calls ): $500
    Transport New York port - Syracuse Warehouse price on invoice: $1500
    Banking fees cost on invoice: $4000
    Total Costs: $83000
    BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT SRL 10% commission fee : $83000 * 0.1 = S8300
    Total without Romanian 19% VAT: $91300
    Total Romanian 19% VAT: $17347
    Total your company needs to send to BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT SRL: $91300 + $17347 = $108647
    When products arrive at your Syracuse Warehouse, you or your legal company representative inspect the products. If the products are according to commission contract, your company representative signs the handover documents and BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT SRL transfers payments to suppliers involved. Task completed !

    and other expenses ( unknown costs is called systematic risk )

    * goods of group 233 (Preparations used in animal feeding; lucerne (alfalfa) meal and pellets)

    Note: For all products in this group, your company has to send the technical specs / quality parameters

    Note: Your company must be authorised to buy this products. ( We do not accept requests from speculators )

    Note: Suppliers for products in this group must be authorized by food safety organisations and must have proof of HACCP plan or HACCP accredited certificate

    Note: Products in this category must be pasteurized or sterilized and packaged according to food safety standards in recyclable or biodegradable food grade packaging

    Note: Frozen* means between -20 and -18° C, Cold* means between 0 and 4° C, Cool* means between 8 and 15° C, Room temperature* means between 15 and 20° C

    Note: The relative humidity (RH) must be under or equal to maximum allowed by exporter-importer governments, the products must be transpored and stored according to manufacturer's instructions

    Note: Exporting - importing meat and animal byproducts is very complex. e.g. Only a few countries are allowed to import meat and animal byproducts inside the EU

    Note: We do not accept suppliers from regions with disease outbreaks. ( That means if you have diseases like Covid, Ebola virus, Swine flu, Mad Cow disease in your region we will not accept any meat or animal origin products from your company, even if your government tells us there is no problem, we must verify. )

    Note: For all products in this group, your company has to send the technical specs / quality parameters

    Note: Suppliers for products in this group must be authorized by food safety organisations and must have proof of HACCP plan or HACCP accredited certificate

    Note: Products in this category must be pasteurized or sterilized and packaged according to food safety standards in recyclable or biodegradable food grade packaging

    Note: Frozen* means between -20 and -18° C, Cold* means between 2 and 4° C, Cool* means between 8 and 15° C, Room temperature* means between 15 and 20° C

    Note: The relative humidity (RH) must be under or equal to maximum allowed by exporter-importer governments, the products must be transpored and stored according to manufacturer's instructions

    Note: Exporting - importing meat and animal byproducts is very complex. e.g. Only a few countries are allowed to import meat and animal byproducts inside the EU

    Note: We do not accept suppliers from regions with disease outbreaks. ( That means if you have diseases like Covid, Ebola virus, Swine flu, Mad Cow disease in your region we will not accept any meat or animal origin products from your company, even if your government tells us there is no problem, we must verify. )

    Note: For all products in this group, your company has to send the technical specs / quality parameters

    Note: Your company must be authorised to buy this products. ( We do not accept requests from speculators )

    Note: Suppliers for products in this group must be authorized by food safety organisations and must have proof of HACCP plan or HACCP accredited certificate

    Note: Products in this category must be pasteurized or sterilized and packaged according to food safety standards in recyclable or biodegradable food grade packaging

    Note: Frozen* means between -20 and -18° C, Cold* means between 0 and 4° C, Cool* means between 8 and 15° C, Room temperature* means between 15 and 20° C

    Note: The relative humidity (RH) must be under or equal to maximum allowed by exporter-importer governments, the products must be transpored and stored according to manufacturer's instructions

The brine is a solution of potable water and food-grade salt (CXS 150-1985) with zero additives. Supplies must also have document proof that the water is "drinking - potable water". Suppliers can get the public drinking water lab test from the local water company or from the Mayor's office. When the food agency of the country where the products are imported tests the brine and if they discover that the water is not drinking water, the supplier will not get payed and his products will be confiscated and destroyed. All suppliers must have legal documents proof that shows their products are safe.If the border guards consider that the olives are cured, they will classify the goods as 200570

    200110 - Vegetable preparations; cucumbers and gherkins, prepared or preserved by vinegar or acetic acid

    BSEI-200110-0003 Room temperature* - Fresh whole gherkins preserved by vinegar with zero additives - for human consumption ( Cucumis sativus )

    Explanatory note for BSEI-200110: The fresh cucumbers and gherkins must be preserved by vinegar according to Standard CXS 66-1981. The supplier can add the following ingredients: [ cucumbers or gherkins, potable water, vinegar, food grade salt, vegetable oils, paprika, herbs, spices, condiments, sugar or honey, mustard seeds ] and no additives. Vegetables shall not exceed 5% of the total weight of the product. Mustard seeds shall not exceed 30% of total weight of the product.

    Explanatory note for BSEI-200570: The fresh olives will be preserved according to Standard CXS 66-1981 in brine. Clients do not need to wait for olives to cure before they can use them, this are olives ready to eat. The brine is a solution of potable water and food-grade salt (CXS 150-1985) with zero additives. Supplies must also have document proof that the water is "drinking - potable water". Suppliers can get the public drinking water lab test from the local water company or from the Mayor's office. When the food agency of the country where the products are imported tests the brine and if they discover that the water is not drinking water, the supplier will not get payed and his products will be confiscated and destroyed. All suppliers must have legal documents proof that shows their products are safe.

    * goods of group 214 (Prepared and preserved fruits and nuts)

    Note: For all products in this group, your company has to send the technical specs / quality parameters

    Note: Your company must be authorised to buy this products. ( We do not accept requests from speculators )

    Note: Suppliers for products in this group must be authorized by food safety organisations and must have proof of HACCP plan or HACCP accredited certificate

    Note: Products in this category must be pasteurized or sterilized and packaged according to food safety standards in recyclable or biodegradable food grade packaging

    Note: Frozen* means between -20 and -18° C, Cold* means between 0 and 4° C, Cool* means between 8 and 15° C, Room temperature* means between 15 and 20° C

    Note: The relative humidity (RH) must be under or equal to maximum allowed by exporter-importer governments, the products must be transpored and stored according to manufacturer's instructions

    Note: Products in this category must be pasteurized or sterilized and packaged according to food safety standards in recyclable or biodegradable food grade packaging

    Note: We do not accept suppliers from regions with disease outbreaks.     Explanatory note for BSEI-040610, BSEI-040640, BSEI-040690: Company client - Wait a minute, why should i buy cheese from Europe ? i can make my own European cheese. I just need the recipe. To obtain the same taste, you need the grass, the animals, the rennet, the water, the air from these countries, also the skilled workers. Geographical indications establish intellectual property rights for specific products, whose qualities are specifically linked to the area of production.

    61223 - Wholesale trade services on a fee or contract basis, of meat, poultry and game
    Download as PDF

    * goods of group 211 (Meat and meat products)

    Note: For all products in this group, your company has to send the technical specs / quality parameters

    Note: Your company must be authorised to buy this products. ( We do not accept requests from speculators )

    Note: Suppliers for products in this group must be authorized by food safety organisations and must have proof of HACCP plan or HACCP accredited certificate

    Note: Products in this category must be pasteurized or sterilized and packaged according to food safety standards in recyclable or biodegradable food grade packaging

    Note: Frozen* means between -20 and -18° C, Cold* means between 2 and 4° C, Cool* means between 8 and 15° C, Room temperature* means between 15 and 20° C

    Note: The relative humidity (RH) must be under or equal to maximum allowed by exporter-importer governments, the products must be transpored and stored according to manufacturer's instructions

    Note: Exporting - importing meat and animal byproducts is very complex. e.g. Only a few countries are allowed to import meat and animal byproducts inside the EU

    Note: We do not accept suppliers from regions with disease outbreaks. ( That means if you have disease like Covid, Ebola virus, Swine flu, Mad Cow disease in your region we will not accept any meat or animal origin products from your company, even if your government tells us there is no problem, we must verify. )

    Note: For all products in this category you must have documents that you raised, feed, slaughter, proccesed the animals according to international food safety - food hygiene - biosecurity standards. The animals can be slaughter and stunned or the client company must send their own butchers to slaughter the animals according to their religios believes e.g. Kosher, Halal and so on. Universal Declaration of Human Rights Article 18 - Everyone has the right to freedom of thought, conscience and religion.

    Note: Do not contact us to send you live animals. It's cruel to transport animals long distance. If you want to raise animals we can send you fodder.

    Note: We do not accept meat from sick or infected animals, animals allowed to eat garbage, abused or bruised or injured animals, newly born, pregnant animals, animals with calfs under 1 year, animals with high fat deposits, stressed animals, uncastrated male animals, castrated under 4 months male animals, not well rested animals during the 24-hour period before slaughter, animals handled with electric prodders, animals living in unhygienic and overcrowded conditions, live animals not transported in clean-disinfected-washed-ventilated specialized vehicles, live animals transported in overcrowded vehicles, live animals transported more then 50-100km from place of origin.

    Note: The meat must be washed only with potable water, the meat should not have blood marks and must be clean, the meat must not have any forign smell, the meat must not have broken bones, the meat must not be bruised, the meat must not be discolored, the meat must have characteristic color and so on, the meat must have the mandatory food safety and legal documents according to the international legislation and national legislation of each country.

    Note: Meat is considered a biological weapon. Before we release any payment for these products, we want the legal representative of the supplier, his wife, his kids and his family to cook and eat a meat sample from the same lot that is shipped to clients around the world.

    Note: Meat should be exported as a last resort. Fodder does not need expensive cold chain transport and logistics.

If you have a restaurant and if you need fresh non-frozen meat your company needs to be close to a slaughterhouse also. Transporting fresh non-frozen meat long distance is not efficient. When they will invent commercial vehicles that run on free electricity then we can transport Cold* meat long distance.

    k) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. is not a food operator and DOES NOT NEED a HACCP certificate, HACCP plan or ISO 22000, we only order the food from your companies and we find authorized transporters to transport the food if client companies can not transport it.     Warranty Info

    For products, example electronics and electrical items that we have in catalog we can not give warranty.

    The warranty is valid only in the country where the product is bought.

    For some products that we buy from merchants and producers, we can only open the packages, test them if they are functional before we send them to your company, and we can also ask the suppliers to replace them before we send them to you.

    We will add a clause in the contract that these "products" will be sent to you without warranty

    For some products we will try to find suppliers that offer international warranty.

    Banned Synthetic Food Additives

    In our opinion, all synthetic food additives are bad.


    Food additives are chemicals you eat, same as you swallow medicines.


    If you request products that must contain synthetic food additives, we will reject to collaborate with you.



    Regulation (EC) No 1333/2008 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 16 December 2008 on food additives



    Article 3 - Definitions


    (a) ‘food additive’ shall mean any substance not normally consumed as a food in itself and not normally used as a characteristic ingredient of food, whether or not it has nutritive value, the intentional addition of which to food for a technological purpose in the manufacture, processing, preparation, treatment, packaging, transport or storage of such food results, or may be reasonably expected to result, in it or its by-products becoming directly or indirectly a component of such foods;

    The following are not considered to be food additives:

    (i) monosaccharides, disaccharides or oligosaccharides and foods containing these substances used for their sweetening properties;

    (ii) foods, whether dried or in concentrated form, including flavourings incorporated during the manufacturing of compound foods, because of their aromatic, sapid or nutritive properties together with a secondary colouring effect;

    (iii) substances used in covering or coating materials, which do not form part of foods and are not intended to be consumed together with those foods;

    (iv) products containing pectin and derived from dried apple pomace or peel of citrus fruits or quinces, or from a mixture of them, by the action of dilute acid followed by partial neutralisation with sodium or potassium salts (liquid pectin);

    (v) chewing gum bases;

    (vi) white or yellow dextrin, roasted or dextrinated starch, starch modified by acid or alkali treatment, bleached starch, physically modified starch and starch treated by amylolitic enzymes;

    (vii) ammonium chloride;

    (viii) blood plasma, edible gelatin, protein hydrolysates and their salts, milk protein and gluten;

    (ix) amino acids and their salts other than glutamic acid, glycine, cysteine and cystine and their salts having no technological function;

    (x) caseinates and casein;

    (xi) inulin;


    (b) ‘processing aid’ shall mean any substance which:

    (i) is not consumed as a food by itself;

    (ii) is intentionally used in the processing of raw materials, foods or their ingredients, to fulfil a certain technological purpose during treatment or processing; and

    (iii) may result in the unintentional but technically unavoidable presence in the final product of residues of the substance or its derivatives provided they do not present any health risk and do not have any technological effect on the final product;


    (c) ‘functional class’ shall mean one of the categories set out in Annex I based on the technological function a food additive exerts in the foodstuff;


    (d) ‘unprocessed food’ shall mean a food which has not undergone any treatment resulting in a substantial change in the original state of the food, for which purpose the following in particular are not regarded as resulting in substantial change: dividing, parting, severing, boning, mincing, skinning, paring, peeling, grinding, cutting, cleaning, trimming, deep-freezing, freezing, chilling, milling, husking, packing or unpacking;


    (e) ‘food with no added sugars’ shall mean a food without the following:

    (i) any added monosaccharides or disaccharides;

    (ii) any added food containing monosaccharides or disaccharides which is used for its sweetening properties;


    (f) ‘energy-reduced food’ shall mean a food with an energy value reduced by at least 30 % compared with the original food or a similar product;


    (g) ‘table-top sweeteners’ shall mean preparations of permitted sweeteners, which may contain other food additives and/or food ingredients and which are intended for sale to the final consumer as a substitute for sugars;


    (h) ‘quantum satis’ shall mean that no maximum numerical level is specified and substances shall be used in accordance with good manufacturing practice, at a level not higher than is necessary to achieve the intended purpose and provided the consumer is not misled.


    ANNEX I - Functional classes of food additives in foods and of food additives in food additives and food enzymes

    sweeteners are substances used to impart a sweet taste to foods or in table-top sweeteners;

    colours are substances which add or restore colour in a food, and include natural constituents of foods and natural sources which are normally not consumed as foods as such and not normally used as characteristic ingredients of food. Preparations obtained from foods and other edible natural source materials obtained by physical and/or chemical extraction resulting in a selective extraction of the pigments relative to the nutritive or aromatic constituents are colours within the meaning of this Regulation;

    preservatives are substances which prolong the shelf-life of foods by protecting them against deterioration caused by micro-organisms and/or which protect against growth of pathogenic micro-organisms;

    antioxidants are substances which prolong the shelf-life of foods by protecting them against deterioration caused by oxidation, such as fat rancidity and colour changes;

    carriers are substances used to dissolve, dilute, disperse or otherwise physically modify a food additive or a flavouring, food enzyme, nutrient and/or other substance added for nutritional or physiological purposes to a food without altering its function (and without exerting any technological effect themselves) in order to facilitate its handling, application or use;

    acids are substances which increase the acidity of a foodstuff and/or impart a sour taste to it;

    acidity regulators are substances which alter or control the acidity or alkalinity of a foodstuff;

    anti-caking agents are substances which reduce the tendency of individual particles of a foodstuff to adhere to one another;

    anti-foaming agents are substances which prevent or reduce foaming;

    bulking agents are substances which contribute to the volume of a foodstuff without contributing significantly to its available energy value;

    emulsifiers are substances which make it possible to form or maintain a homogenous mixture of two or more immiscible phases such as oil and water in a foodstuff;

    emulsifying salts are substances which convert proteins contained in cheese into a dispersed form and thereby bring about homogenous distribution of fat and other components;

    firming agents are substances which make or keep tissues of fruit or vegetables firm or crisp, or interact with gelling agents to produce or strengthen a gel;

    flavour enhancers are substances which enhance the existing taste and/or odour of a foodstuff;

    foaming agents are substances which make it possible to form a homogenous dispersion of a gaseous phase in a liquid or solid foodstuff;

    gelling agents are substances which give a foodstuff texture through formation of a gel;

    glazing agents (including lubricants) are substances which, when applied to the external surface of a foodstuff, impart a shiny appearance or provide a protective coating;

    humectants are substances which prevent foods from drying out by counteracting the effect of an atmosphere having a low degree of humidity, or promote the dissolution of a powder in an aqueous medium;

    modified starches are substances obtained by one or more chemical treatments of edible starches, which may have undergone a physical or enzymatic treatment, and may be acid or alkali thinned or bleached;

    packaging gases are gases other than air, introduced into a container before, during or after the placing of a foodstuff in that container;

    propellants are gases other than air which expel a foodstuff from a container;

    raising agents are substances or combinations of substances which liberate gas and thereby increase the volume of a dough or a batter;

    sequestrants are substances which form chemical complexes with metallic ions;

    stabilisers are substances which make it possible to maintain the physico-chemical state of a foodstuff; stabilisers include substances which enable the maintenance of a homogenous dispersion of two or more immiscible substances in a foodstuff, substances which stabilise, retain or intensify colour of a foodstuff and substances which increase the binding capacity of the food, including the formation of cross-links between proteins enabling the binding of food pieces into re-constituted food;

    thickeners are substances which increase the viscosity of a foodstuff;

    flour treatment agents are substances, other than emulsifiers, which are added to flour or dough to improve its baking quality;

    contrast enhancers are substances which, when applied to the external surface of fruit or vegetables following depigmentation of predefined parts (e.g. by laser treatment), help to distinguish these parts from the remaining surface by imparting colour following interaction with certain components of the epidermis."

    Countries for which EU banks want supporting documents

    Banks want legal documents before they allow transactions with companies from countries in this list

    - The contract
    - Invoice / invoices, to cover the value of the transaction
    - Certificate of origin issued by the competent authority of the country (or an equivalent document that certifies both the country of the producer and his company name )
    - Inspection certificates ( e.g. phytosanitary certificate / health - veterinary certificate and so on )
    - Declaration / certificate of conformity with technical documentation proof
    - Laboratory analysis proof that shows the products are safe and according to EU standards
    - Transport documents
    - The banks may request additional information/documents to clarify the purpose and nature of transactions

    Recalls

    Proof Documents that we payed excise duties to producers in Romania

    All proofs that we payed excise duties to producers in Romania we will be put here. ( For clients who want to buy this type of products )


    Note: Excise duties products we will buy only from Romania and will not be exported outside European Union for now

    Note: We will import coffee with excise duties from other countries outside the EU only if clients request these products./b>
    In the case of excise duties products ( example bioethanol for fuel use ) in Romania the procedure in this moment in time is this:

    1. The producer ( authorized warehouse ) issues a proforma invoice to the Buyer

    2. The buyer pays the excise duties to the producer ( authorized warehouse ) via bank transfer or money order or via other types of bank payment methods and at details he writes "payment product and payment excise duties value x RON"

    3. The producer ( authorized warehouse ) he will also issue proof that the buyer paid the product including the excise duties , if the producer refuses to issue the proof the authorities must be notified immediately

    4. In case of BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. we will put all this proofs that excise duties have been payed to the producer ( authorized warehouse ) on our website, so anyone that wishes to see them will see them

    5. If the product is outside Romania, Excise duties will be payed again in the country of destination ( it depends on the legislation of that country ) , after that we must request reimbursement of excise duties from Romania and the money will be returned to the client who payed it, the bank fees will be payed by the client also.

    How to Become a Supplier

    To become a supplier you must send us:

    - Document proof that you have legal documents
    - Document proof that the products are safe / high quality
    - Document proof that your products can be repaired and that they have interchangeable parts
    - Document proof that your products can be recycled or that they are biodegradable
    - Document proof that your products do not come from deforested areas
    - Document proof that your company is environment friendly
    - Document proof that your company is sustainable
    - Document proof that your company uses renewable energy
    - Document proof that you respect your workers
    - Document proof that you have production capacity
    - Document proof that you respect intellectual property rights
    - Agreement that you allow us to make public all documents you send
    - Agreement for exclusive rights to buy your products
    and so on
